ARIE vol.038, 1915-1916


A.--List of copper-plates examined during 1915-16.
1
Placement
The trustee of the Veṅkaṭēś-vara temple at Nandyal(Kurnool district).
Year
Vijayanagara
King
Vīrapratāpa Śrīraṅgarāya-dēva-Mahārāya, rulingfrom Penugoṇḍa.
Date
Śaka 1569,Sarvajit,Vaiśākha, śu.15.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Registers that, for the merit of HazaratiKhāna Khāna-Sāhēbulavāru, the nāḍigēru,sthaḷa-paṭṭaṇa-reḍḍis, tōṁṭa-śeṭṭis andkaraṇams of the Peda-Nandyāla-śīmaincluded in Peḍakaṇṭi-śīma, granted to acertain Timmaya, the son of chapparam-dāsari Saruvaya, specified contributionof fees from the several professional com-munities of Nandyāla and from about 70villages of the same sīma for conductingthe chapparam-service of the god Veṅ-kaṭēśa.
2
Placement
Do. do.
Year
Do.
King
Do. do.
Date
Do.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
This is a duplicate of No. 1 with a differ-ence in the order in which the severalvillages are mentioned and in the amountsof contributions.
3
Placement
M.R.Ry. Jarubula Venkates-varlu, village munsif, San-taravuru, (Bapatla taluk,Guntūr district).
Year
Pallava
King
Mahārāja Vijaya-Skandavar-man (II).
Date
33rd year ofreign; Hēman-ta-paksha,tṛitīyā trayō-daśī.
Language and Script
Sanskṛit (in Telugu)
Remarks
Records that the king gave to Gōlaśarmanof the Kāśyapa-gōtra, the village ofO1ṁgōḍu in Karmm[ā]-rāshṭra as a brahma-dēya with the 18 kinds of exemptions.
4
Placement
Do. do.
Year
Do.
King
Pallava-Dharma-MahārājaSimhavarman.
Date
4th year ofreign; Vaiśā-kha, śu[kla]-paksha, pañchami.
Language and Script
Sanskṛit (in Telugu)
Remarks
Registers that the king gave on the occa-sion of the grahaṇa (eclipse), the village ofO1ṁgōḍu in Karmmā-rāshṭra, to a certainDēvaśarman who was a resident of Kuṇḍūrand belonged to the Kāśyapa-gōtra.
5
Placement
M.R.Ry. Javvadi Nagayya,Edavalli (Narasaraopettaluk, Guntūr district).
Year
Kōṭa
King
Mahāmaṇḍalēśvara Manma,Manma-Kēta or Kōṭa-Kēta,(i.e., Kēta III), ‘lord of thecity of Dhānyakaṭaka.’
Date
Śaka 1162,Māgha, Ardhō-daya.
Language and Script
Sanskṛit & Telugu
Remarks
Registers that the king made a gift of thevillage Eḍavalli which was 300 khaṇḍu-kas in extent, dividing it equally amongthe Brāhmaṇas of both the Shaṭsahasracountry and the Vēṅgī country. Gifts ofland in the village were also made tocertain temples.
6
Placement
The priest of the Mukhaliṅga-svāmin temple at Muktes-varam (same taluk anddistrict).
Year
…
King
…
Date
Śaka 1712,Saumya,Āshāḍha,śu. 15.
Language and Script
Telugu
Remarks
Registers that, for the daily worship andofferings of the god Parasavēdēśvarasvāminat Chennupalle, the kāpus and karaṇamsof that village, with the sanction of theMahārājaśrī Hanarabbul-Kumpinī (i.e.the Honourable East India Company)according to the Sanad of the prosperousMr. Rao and with the consent of RājaśrīGuṇṭupalli Narasiṅgarāyaniṅgāru gave 4gorrus of land together with their ownśelagamēras.
7
Placement
M.R.Ry. Rama Reddi, villagemunsif of Dayyamdinne(Adōni taluk, Bellarydistrict).
Year
WesternChalukya.
King
Vinayāditya Satyāśraya
Date
Śaka 614, ex-pired; 12thyear of reigncurrent;Āshāḍha, full-moon, summersolstice (dak-shiṇāyana).
Language and Script
Sanskṛit (in Kanarese)
Remarks
Registers that, at the request of a certainMarddakāri, the king while camping atTaḷayakhēṭa-grāma, made a gift of 200nivartanas of land on the eastern andsouthern sides of the village of Uḷchaḍ inNaḷavāḍi-vishaya, to four Brāhmaṇas.Taḷayakhēṭa is stated to have beensituated near to the north bank of theriver Tagara.

138
Placement
On a slab set up in the courtyard of theŚīrgāḷinātha temple at Sittalundur(Tiruchchengode taluk, Salem district).
Year
Vijayanagara
King
Vīrapratāpa Kṛishṇarāya-Mahārāya, ‘whowas pleased to take every country.’
Date
Śaka 1455 (mis-take for 1445)Svabhānu,Kārttika 23,paurṇimā,Sunday.
Language and Script
Tamil
Remarks

Kanarese
Remarks
Registers that the chief queen Maleyamatidēvī, at therequest of the Daṇḍanāyaka Śrīdharayya, gave tothe 140 mahājanas of Tumbuḷa (in Sindavāḍi-nāḍu)which belonged to her, 30 gadyāṇas of gold fromthe Siddhāya of that village for the maintenance ofthe commentator (on Śāstras), the reader of thePurāṇas, the teacher of the Ṛig-Vēda and theYajur-Vēda and of the Brāhmana in charge of theAgnishṭage.

Language and Script
Kanarese (verse & prose)
Remarks
Evidently the slab belongs to the village of PeddaTumbalam. Gives a genealogical account of thechiefs Brahma (Bammidēva), his son Padmidēvaand Vatsarāja the maternal uncle of the latter.Padmidēvarasa and Vatsarāja were ruling thewhole of the eastern country including Sindavāḍi.The village Kantarike in Bāgi 12, a sub-divisionof Sindavāḍi-one-thousand, was granted to thetemple of Brahmēśvaradēva (at Kaṟekaṇṭhapura inKīrtinārāyaṇapura, the capital of the Sindavāḍiprovince) which had been built by the merchantŚrōtriya Eṟeyama-seṭṭi.

Registers a gift of land by the king tothe temple of Piṇakkaṟukku-Mahādēva at Malai-yaḍikkurichchi, the southern hamlet of Parān-taka-chaturvēdimaṅgalam, a brahmadēya inĀri-nāḍu. When ordering the grant, the kingwas in his palace at Tirunelvēli in Kīḻvēmba-nāḍu.Mentions Vīrapāṇḍiyan Pilāṟu and the seat calledMuṉaiyadaraiyaṉ. Below this is an incompleterecord dated in the 11th year, probably, of the sameking.
